271        protected static String getAreaName(List<String> V)
272        {
273                V=new XVector<String>(V);
274                // find area line first
275                String areaName="";
276                final String firstLine=nextLine(V);
277                if((firstLine.indexOf('~')>=0)&&(firstLine.indexOf('}')>=0))
278                {
279                        String areaLine=firstLine;
280                        areaLine=areaLine.substring(0,areaLine.length()-1);
281                        int x=areaLine.indexOf('}');
282                        areaLine=areaLine.substring(x+1).trim();
283                        x=areaLine.indexOf("  ");
284                        if(x>0)
285                                areaLine=areaLine.substring(x+1).trim();
286                        areaName=areaLine;
287                }
288                else
289                if((firstLine.indexOf('~')>=0)
290                &&(firstLine.startsWith("#AREA "))
291                &&(firstLine.toUpperCase().indexOf(".ARE")<0))
292                {
293                        String areaLine=firstLine;
294                        areaLine=areaLine.substring(5).trim();
295                        if(areaLine.endsWith("~"))
296                                areaLine=areaLine.substring(0,areaLine.length()-1).trim();
297                        areaName=areaLine;
298                }
299                else
300                if(V.size()>1)
301                {
302                        String lineAfter=V.get(1);
303                        if(lineAfter.indexOf('~')<0)
304                                return "";
305                        lineAfter=lineAfter.substring(0,lineAfter.length()-1);
306                        if((lineAfter.indexOf(".are")>=0)&&(V.size()>2)&&(lineAfter.indexOf("@@")<0))
307                        {
308                                lineAfter=V.get(2);
309                                if(lineAfter.indexOf('~')<0)
310                                        return "";
311                                lineAfter=lineAfter.substring(0,lineAfter.length()-1).trim();
312                                if(lineAfter.length()>0)
313                                        areaName=lineAfter.trim();
314                                else
315                                if(V.size()>3)
316                                {
317                                        lineAfter=V.get(3);
318                                        if(lineAfter.indexOf('~')<0)
319                                                return "";
320                                        if(lineAfter.endsWith("~"))
321                                                lineAfter=lineAfter.substring(0,lineAfter.length()-1);
322                                        final int x=lineAfter.indexOf('}');
323                                        if(x>0)
324                                                lineAfter=lineAfter.substring(x+1).trim();
325                                        if(CMParms.numBits(lineAfter)>1)
326                                                areaName=CMParms.getPastBit(lineAfter,0);
327                                        else
328                                                areaName=lineAfter;
329                                }
330                        }
331                        else
332                                areaName=lineAfter.trim();
333                }
334                if(areaName.toUpperCase().startsWith("NAME "))
335                {
336                        if((areaName.length()>=41)
337                        &&(areaName.charAt(12)=='{')
338                        &&(areaName.charAt(21)!=' ')
339                        &&(areaName.charAt(40)==' '))
340                                areaName=areaName.substring(21,41).trim();
341                        else
342                        if((areaName.length()>13)&&((areaName.charAt(12)=='{')||(areaName.charAt(13)=='{')))
343                        {
344                                final int x=areaName.indexOf('}',12);
345                                if(x>12)
346                                        areaName=areaName.substring(x+1).trim();
347                                else
348                                        areaName=areaName.substring(5).trim();
349                        }
350                        else
351                                areaName=areaName.substring(5).trim();
352                }
353
354                if((areaName.indexOf(""+((char)27))>=0)
355                ||(areaName.indexOf('&')>=0)
356                ||(areaName.indexOf('{')>=0)
357                ||(areaName.indexOf("@@")>=0))
358                {
359                        for (final String[] color : colors)
360                                if(areaName.indexOf(color[0])>=0)
361                                        areaName=CMStrings.replaceAll(areaName,color[0],color[1]);
362                }
363                return CMStrings.removeColors(CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(areaName));
364        }
365
366        protected static Room getRoom(java.util.Map<String, Room> hashedRoomSet, String areaName, String calledThis)
367        {
368                if(calledThis.startsWith("#"))
369                {
370                        while(calledThis.startsWith("#0")&&(calledThis.length()>2))
371                                calledThis="#"+calledThis.substring(2);
372                        if(hashedRoomSet.containsKey(areaName+calledThis))
373                                return hashedRoomSet.get(areaName+calledThis);
374                        for(final String key : hashedRoomSet.keySet())
375                                if(key.endsWith(calledThis))
376                                        return hashedRoomSet.get(key);
377                }
378                else
379                if(calledThis.startsWith(areaName+"#"))
380                {
381                        while(calledThis.startsWith(areaName+"#0")&&(calledThis.length()>(areaName.length()+2)))
382                                calledThis=areaName+"#"+calledThis.substring(areaName.length()+2);
383                        if(hashedRoomSet.containsKey(calledThis))
384                                return hashedRoomSet.get(calledThis);
385                }
386                while(calledThis.startsWith("0")&&(calledThis.length()>1))
387                        calledThis=calledThis.substring(1);
388                if(hashedRoomSet.containsKey(calledThis))
389                        return hashedRoomSet.get(calledThis);
390                for(final String key : hashedRoomSet.keySet())
391                {
392                        if(key.endsWith("#"+calledThis))
393                                return hashedRoomSet.get(key);
394                }
395                return null;
396        }
397
398        protected static Room getRoom(Map<String, Room> areaHashedRoomSet, Map<String, Room> hashedRoomSet, String areaName, String calledThis)
399        {
400                Room R=null;
401                if(areaHashedRoomSet!=null)
402                        R=getRoom(areaHashedRoomSet,areaName,calledThis);
403                if(R!=null)
404                        return R;
405                R=getRoom(hashedRoomSet,areaName,calledThis);
406                if(R!=null)
407                        return R;
408                return CMLib.map().getRoom(areaName+"#"+calledThis);
409        }
410
411        protected static void processRoomRelinks(List<String> reLinkTable, String areaName, Map<String, Room> areaHashedRoomSet, Map<String, Room> hashedRoomSet)
412        {
413                // try to re-link olde room links
414                if(reLinkTable!=null)
415                {
416                        for(int r=0;r<reLinkTable.size();r++)
417                        {
418                                final String link=reLinkTable.get(r);
419                                String nextLink="";
420                                if(r<(reLinkTable.size()-1))
421                                        nextLink=reLinkTable.get(r+1);
422                                final int s1=link.indexOf('/');
423                                final int s2=link.lastIndexOf('/');
424                                final String sourceRoomID=link.substring(0,s1);
425                                synchronized(("SYNC"+sourceRoomID).intern())
426                                {
427                                        final int direction=CMath.s_int(link.substring(s1+1,s2));
428                                        final String destRoomID=link.substring(s2+1);
429                                        final Room sourceRoom=getRoom(areaHashedRoomSet,hashedRoomSet,areaName,sourceRoomID);
430                                        final Room destRoom=getRoom(areaHashedRoomSet,hashedRoomSet,areaName,destRoomID);
431                                        if((sourceRoom==null)||(destRoom==null))
432                                                Log.errOut("Import","Relink error: "+sourceRoomID+"="+sourceRoom+"/"+destRoomID+"="+destRoom);
433                                        else
434                                        {
435                                                sourceRoom.rawDoors()[direction]=destRoom;
436                                                if(((!hashedRoomSet.containsValue(sourceRoom)))
437                                                &&((nextLink.length()==0)||(!nextLink.startsWith(sourceRoomID+"/"))))
438                                                        CMLib.database().DBUpdateExits(sourceRoom);
439                                        }
440                                }
441                        }
442                }
443        }
444
445        protected boolean temporarilyDeleteArea(MOB mob, List<String> reLinkTable, String areaName)
446        {
447                if((mob!=null)&&(CMLib.flags().isInTheGame(mob,true)&&(mob.location().getArea().Name().equalsIgnoreCase(areaName))))
448                {
449                        mob.tell(L("You dip!  You are IN that area!  Leave it first..."));
450                        return false;
451                }
452                try
453                {
454                        for(final Enumeration<Room> r=CMLib.map().rooms();r.hasMoreElements();)
455                        {
456                                final Room R=r.nextElement();
457                                if(!R.getArea().Name().equalsIgnoreCase(areaName))
458                                {
459                                        for(int d=Directions.NUM_DIRECTIONS()-1;d>=0;d--)
460                                        {
461                                                final Room dirR=R.rawDoors()[d];
462                                                if((dirR!=null)&&(dirR.getArea().Name().equalsIgnoreCase(areaName)))
463                                                        reLinkTable.add(R.roomID()+"/"+d+"/"+dirR.roomID());
464                                        }
465                                }
466                        }
467                }
468                catch(final NoSuchElementException e)
469                {
470                }
471                while(true)
472                {
473                        Room foundOne=null;
474                        try
475                        {
476                                for(final Enumeration<Room> r=CMLib.map().rooms();r.hasMoreElements();)
477                                {
478                                        final Room R=r.nextElement();
479                                        if(R.getArea().Name().equalsIgnoreCase(areaName))
480                                        {
481                                                foundOne=R;
482                                                break;
483                                        }
484                                }
485                        }
486                        catch (final NoSuchElementException e)
487                        {
488                        }
489                        if(foundOne==null)
490                                break;
491                        CMLib.map().obliterateMapRoom(foundOne);
492                }
493                final Area A1=CMLib.map().getArea(areaName);
494                if(A1!=null)
495                {
496                        CMLib.database().DBDeleteArea(A1);
497                        CMLib.map().delArea(A1);
498                }
499                return true;
500        }
501
502        protected static String getAreaAuthor(List<String> V)
503        {
504                V=new XVector<String>(V);
505                for(int v=0;v<V.size();v++)
506                {
507                        String s=V.get(v).trim();
508                        if(s.toUpperCase().startsWith("#AUTHOR "))
509                        {
510                                s=s.substring(8).trim();
511                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
512                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
513                                return s;
514                        }
515                        else
516                        if(s.toUpperCase().startsWith("BUILDERS "))
517                        {
518                                s=s.substring(9).trim();
519                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
520                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
521                                if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
522                                        continue;
523                                return s;
524                        }
525                        else
526                        if((s.toUpperCase().startsWith("NAME     "))
527                        &&(s.indexOf('{')>0))
528                        {
529                                s=s.substring(5).trim();
530                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
531                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
532                                if(CMParms.parse(s).size()>0)
533                                        s=CMParms.parse(s).lastElement();
534                                if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
535                                        continue;
536                                return s;
537                        }
538                        else
539                        if((s.toUpperCase().startsWith("#AREA "))
540                        &&(s.indexOf('{')>0))
541                        {
542                                s=s.substring(6).trim();
543                                if(s.trim().startsWith("{"))
544                                {
545                                        int x=s.trim().indexOf('}');
546                                        if(x>0)
547                                                s=s.substring(x+1).trim();
548                                        if(s.endsWith("~"))
549                                                s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
550                                        x=s.indexOf(' ');
551                                        if((x>1)
552                                        &&(s.substring(0,x).trim().toUpperCase().equals("THE"))
553                                        &&(CMParms.parse(s).size()>0))
554                                                s=CMParms.parse(s).lastElement();
555                                        else
556                                        if(x>1)
557                                                s=s.substring(0,x).trim();
558                                        if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
559                                                continue;
560                                        return s;
561                                }
562                        }
563                        else
564                        if(s.trim().startsWith("O ")&&(s.trim().endsWith("~")))
565                        {
566                                s=s.substring(1).trim();
567                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
568                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
569                                if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
570                                        continue;
571                                return s;
572                        }
573                        else
574                        if(s.toUpperCase().startsWith("CREDITS "))
575                        {
576                                s=s.substring(8).trim();
577                                if(s.trim().startsWith("("))
578                                        continue;
579                                if(s.trim().startsWith("{"))
580                                {
581                                        final int x=s.trim().indexOf('}');
582                                        if(x>0)
583                                                s=s.substring(x+1).trim();
584                                }
585                                else
586                                if((CMParms.parse(s).size()>2)
587                                &&(CMath.isNumber(CMParms.parse(s).get(0)))
588                                &&(CMath.isNumber(CMParms.parse(s).get(1))))
589                                        s=CMParms.parse(s).get(2);
590                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
591                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
592                                final int x=s.indexOf(' ');
593                                if(x>1)
594                                        s=s.substring(0,x).trim();
595                                if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
596                                        continue;
597                                return s;
598                        }
599                        else
600                        if(s.trim().startsWith("{"))
601                        {
602                                int x=s.trim().indexOf('}');
603                                if(x>0)
604                                        s=s.substring(x+1).trim();
605                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
606                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
607                                x=s.indexOf(' ');
608                                if((x>1)
609                                &&(s.substring(0,x).trim().toUpperCase().equals("THE"))
610                                &&(CMParms.parse(s).size()>0))
611                                        s=CMParms.parse(s).lastElement();
612                                else
613                                if(x>1)
614                                        s=s.substring(0,x).trim();
615                                if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
616                                        continue;
617                                return s;
618                        }
619                        else
620                        if(s.trim().startsWith("["))
621                        {
622                                int x=s.trim().indexOf(']');
623                                if(x>0)
624                                        s=s.substring(x+1).trim();
625                                if(s.endsWith("~"))
626                                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1).trim();
627                                x=s.indexOf(' ');
628                                if((x>1)
629                                &&(s.substring(0,x).trim().toUpperCase().equals("THE"))
630                                &&(CMParms.parse(s).size()>0))
631                                        s=CMParms.parse(s).lastElement();
632                                else
633                                if(x>1)
634                                        s=s.substring(0,x).trim();
635                                if((s.length()==0)||(s.toUpperCase().equalsIgnoreCase("NONE")))
636                                        continue;
637                                return s;
638                        }
639                }
640                return "";
641        }

752        protected static String nextLine(List<String> V)
753        {
754                if(V.size()==0)
755                        return "";
756                return V.get(0);
757        }
758
759        protected static String eatLine(List<String> V)
760        {
761                if(V.size()==0)
762                        return "";
763                final String s=V.get(0);
764                V.remove(0);
765                return s;
766        }
767
768        protected static String eatNextLine(List<String> V)
769        {
770                String s="";
771                while((s.trim().length()==0)&&(V.size()>0))
772                        s=eatLine(V);
773                return s;
774        }

776        protected static Room changeRoomClass(Room R, String newClass)
777        {
778                final Room R2=CMClass.getLocale(newClass);
779                if(R2==null)
780                {
781                        Log.errOut("Import","Cannot find room class "+newClass+".");
782                        return R;
783                }
784                final Area area=R.getArea();
785                if(area!=null)
786                        area.delProperRoom(R);
787                R2.setRoomID(R.roomID());
788                R2.setArea(R.getArea());
789                if(R2.expirationDate()!=0)
790                        R2.setExpirationDate(R2.expirationDate()+(360000));
791                R2.setDescription(R.description());
792                R2.setDisplayText(R.displayText());
793                R2.setName(R.name());
794                R2.setBasePhyStats(R.basePhyStats());
795                R2.setMiscText(R.text());
796                return R2;
797        }

799        protected static long getBitMask(String str, int which)
800        {
801                String s=CMParms.getCleanBit(str,which).trim();
802                if(s.length()==0)
803                        return 0;
804                int x=s.indexOf('|');
805                if((x<0)&&(s.length()>0)&&(CMath.s_int(s)==0))
806                {
807                        boolean otherStyle=true;
808                        long num=0;
809                        for(int z=0;z<s.length();z++)
810                                if(!Character.isLetter(s.charAt(z)))
811                                {
812                                   otherStyle=false;
813                                   break;
814                                }
815                                else
816                                if(Character.isUpperCase(s.charAt(z)))
817                                        num=num|(1<<(s.charAt(z))-('A'));
818                                else
819                                if(Character.isLowerCase(s.charAt(z)))
820                                        num=num|(1<<(26+((s.charAt(z))-('a'))));
821
822                        if(otherStyle)
823                                return num;
824                }
825
826                long num=0;
827                while(x>0)
828                {
829                        num=num|CMath.s_int(s.substring(0,x));
830                        s=s.substring(x+1);
831                        x=s.indexOf('|');
832                }
833
834                return (num|CMath.s_int(s));
835        }
836
837        protected static String trimSpacesOnly(String s)
838        {
839                while(s.startsWith(" ")||s.startsWith("\t")||s.startsWith("\n")||s.startsWith("\r"))
840                        s=s.substring(1);
841                while(s.endsWith(" ")||s.endsWith("\t")||s.endsWith("\n")||s.endsWith("\r"))
842                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1);
843                return s;
844        }
845
846        protected static String eatLineSquiggle(List<String> V)
847        {
848                if(V.size()==0)
849                        return "";
850                String s=eatLine(V);
851                while(s.indexOf('~')<0)
852                {
853                        final String l=eatLine(V);
854                        if(l.startsWith(" "))
855                                s+="%0D"+l;
856                        else
857                        if(l.length()==0)
858                                s+="%0D";
859                        else
860                                s+=" "+l;
861                        if(V.size()==0)
862                                break;
863                }
864                s=trimSpacesOnly(s);
865
866                if(s.startsWith("~") && (s.length()>2) && (s.charAt(1)=='#') && (V.size()>0))
867                {
868                        V.add(0,s.substring(1));
869                        s="~";
870                }
871                if(s.endsWith("~"))
872                        s=s.substring(0,s.length()-1);
873
874                if(s.indexOf('^')>=0)
875                        s=CMStrings.replaceAll(s,"^","^^");
876
877                if((s.indexOf(""+((char)27))>=0)
878                ||(s.indexOf('&')>=0)
879                ||(s.indexOf('{')>=0)
880                ||(s.indexOf('_')>=0)
881                ||(s.indexOf("@@")>=0))
882                {
883                        for (final String[] color : colors)
884                                if(s.indexOf(color[0])>=0)
885                                        s=CMStrings.replaceAll(s,color[0],color[1]);
886                }
887
888                final int x=s.indexOf("@eng");
889                if(x>=0)
890                {
891                        int y=s.indexOf("@rus",x);
892                        if(y<x)
893                                y=s.indexOf("@ger",x);
894                        if(y<x)
895                                y=s.indexOf("@spa",x);
896                        if(y<x)
897                                y=s.length();
898                        s=s.substring(x+4,y);
899                }
900                return s.trim();
901        }

903        protected static boolean hasReadableContent(String objectName)
904        {
905                objectName=objectName.toUpperCase();
906                if((objectName.indexOf("SIGN")>=0)
907                        ||(objectName.indexOf("PLAQUE")>=0)
908                        ||(objectName.indexOf("NOTICE")>=0)
909                        ||(objectName.indexOf("PAPER")>=0)
910                        ||(objectName.indexOf("WRITING")>=0)
911                        ||(objectName.indexOf("CARVING")>=0)
912                        ||(objectName.indexOf("LETTER")>=0)
913                        ||(objectName.indexOf("INSCRIPTION")>=0)
914                        ||(objectName.indexOf("NOTE")>=0)
915                        ||(objectName.indexOf("POST")>=0))
916                                return true;
917                return false;
918        }
919
920        protected static String fixReadableContent(String text)
921        {
922                while(text.startsWith("%0D"))
923                        text=text.substring(3);
924                if((text.toUpperCase().trim().startsWith("IT SAYS `"))
925                ||(text.toUpperCase().trim().startsWith("IT SAYS '")))
926                {
927                        text=text.trim().substring(9).trim();
928                        if((text.endsWith("'"))||(text.endsWith("`")))
929                                text=text.substring(0,text.length()-1);
930                }
931                if(text.toUpperCase().trim().startsWith("IT SAYS:"))
932                        text=text.trim().substring(8).trim();
933                if(text.toUpperCase().trim().startsWith("IT SAYS"))
934                        text=text.trim().substring(7).trim();
935                return text;
936        }

938        protected static boolean returnAnError(Session sess, String str, boolean compileErrors, List<Object> commands)
939        {
940                if((str==null)||(str.length()==0))
941                        return true;
942                Log.errOut("Import",str);
943                if(sess!=null)
944                        sess.println(str);
945                if(compileErrors&&(commands!=null))
946                        commands.add(str);
947                return false;
948        }

950        protected void importCustomFiles(MOB mob, Map<String,String> files, Set<String> customBother, boolean noPrompt, boolean noDelete)
951        throws IOException
952        {
953                if(files.size()==0)
954                        return;
955                if((!noPrompt)&&((mob==null)||(mob.session()==null)))
956                        return;
957                for(final Iterator<String> e=files.keySet().iterator();e.hasNext();)
958                {
959                        String filename=e.next();
960                        final String data=files.get(filename);
961                        if(customBother.contains(filename))
962                                continue;
963
964                        if((!filename.startsWith("//"))&&(!filename.startsWith("::")))
965                        {
966                                if(!filename.startsWith("/"))
967                                        filename="/"+filename;
968                                filename="::"+filename;
969                        }
970
971                        if(new CMFile(filename,mob).exists())
972                        {
973                                if(noDelete)
974                                        continue;
975                                else
976                                if(!noPrompt)
977                                        if(!mob.session().confirm(L("\n\rExternal resource '@x1' found, import (Y/n)?",filename),"Y"))
978                                                continue;
979                        }
980                        Resources.saveFileResource(filename,mob,new StringBuffer(data));
981                }
982        }
983
984        protected void importCustomObjects(MOB mob, List<CMObject> custom, Set<String> customBother, boolean noPrompt, boolean noDelete)
985        throws IOException
986        {
987                if(custom.size()==0)
988                        return;
989                if((!noPrompt)&&((mob==null)||(mob.session()==null)))
990                        return;
991                for(int c=0;c<custom.size();c++)
992                {
993                        if(custom.get(c) instanceof Race)
994                        {
995                                final Race R=(Race)custom.get(c);
996                                if(customBother.contains(R.ID()))
997                                        continue;
998
999                                final Race R2=CMClass.getRace(R.ID());
1000                                if(R2==null)
1001                                {
1002                                        if(!noPrompt)
1003                                        {
1004                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Race '@x1' found, import (Y/n)?",R.ID()),"Y"))
1005                                                        continue;
1006                                        }
1007                                        CMClass.addRace(R);
1008                                        CMLib.database().DBCreateRace(R.ID(),R.racialParms());
1009                                }
1010                                else
1011                                if(!R2.isGeneric())
1012                                {
1013                                        if(noDelete)
1014                                                continue;
1015                                        else
1016                                        if(!noPrompt)
1017                                        {
1018                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Race '@x1' found which would override your standard race.  Import anyway (Y/n)?",R.ID()),"Y"))
1019                                                        continue;
1020                                        }
1021                                        CMClass.addRace(R);
1022                                        CMLib.database().DBCreateRace(R.ID(),R.racialParms());
1023                                }
1024                        }
1025                        else
1026                        if(custom.get(c) instanceof CharClass)
1027                        {
1028                                final CharClass C=(CharClass)custom.get(c);
1029                                if(customBother.contains(C.ID()))
1030                                        continue;
1031
1032                                final CharClass C2=CMClass.getCharClass(C.ID());
1033                                if(C2==null)
1034                                {
1035                                        if(!noPrompt)
1036                                        {
1037                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Char Class '@x1' found, import (Y/n)?",C.ID()),"Y"))
1038                                                        continue;
1039                                        }
1040                                        CMClass.addCharClass(C);
1041                                        CMLib.database().DBCreateClass(C.ID(),C.classParms());
1042                                }
1043                                else
1044                                if(!C2.isGeneric())
1045                                {
1046                                        if(noDelete)
1047                                                continue;
1048                                        else
1049                                        if(!noPrompt)
1050                                        {
1051                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Char Class '@x1' found which would override your standard class.  Import anyway (Y/n)?",C.ID()),"Y"))
1052                                                        continue;
1053                                        }
1054                                        CMClass.addCharClass(C);
1055                                        CMLib.database().DBCreateClass(C.ID(),C.classParms());
1056                                }
1057                        }
1058                        else
1059                        if(custom.get(c) instanceof Ability)
1060                        {
1061                                final Ability A=(Ability)custom.get(c);
1062                                if(customBother.contains(A.ID()))
1063                                        continue;
1064
1065                                final Ability A2=CMClass.getAbility(A.ID());
1066                                if(A2==null)
1067                                {
1068                                        if(!noPrompt)
1069                                        {
1070                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Ability '@x1' found, import (Y/n)?",A.ID()),"Y"))
1071                                                        continue;
1072                                        }
1073                                        CMClass.addClass(CMObjectType.ABILITY, A);
1074                                        CMLib.database().DBCreateAbility(A.ID(),CMClass.getSimpleClassName(A),A.getStat("ALLXML"));
1075                                }
1076                                else
1077                                if(!A2.isGeneric())
1078                                {
1079                                        if(noDelete)
1080                                                continue;
1081                                        else
1082                                        if(!noPrompt)
1083                                        {
1084                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Ability '@x1' found which would override your standard Ability.  Import anyway (Y/n)?",A.ID()),"Y"))
1085                                                        continue;
1086                                        }
1087                                        CMClass.delClass(CMObjectType.ABILITY, A2);
1088                                        CMClass.addClass(CMObjectType.ABILITY, A);
1089                                        CMLib.database().DBCreateAbility(A.ID(),CMClass.getSimpleClassName(A),A.getStat("ALLXML"));
1090                                }
1091                        }
1092                        else
1093                        if(custom.get(c) instanceof Manufacturer)
1094                        {
1095                                final Manufacturer M=(Manufacturer)custom.get(c);
1096                                if(customBother.contains(M.name()))
1097                                        continue;
1098
1099                                final Manufacturer eM=CMLib.tech().getManufacturer(M.name());
1100                                if(eM==null)
1101                                {
1102                                        if(!noPrompt)
1103                                        {
1104                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Manufacturer '@x1' found, import (Y/n)?",M.name()),"Y"))
1105                                                        continue;
1106                                        }
1107                                        CMLib.tech().addManufacturer(eM);
1108                                }
1109                                else
1110                                {
1111                                        if(noDelete)
1112                                                continue;
1113                                        else
1114                                        if(!noPrompt)
1115                                        {
1116                                                if(!mob.session().confirm(L("Custom Manufacturer '@x1' found which would override your existing one.  Import anyway (Y/n)?",M.name()),"Y"))
1117                                                        continue;
1118                                        }
1119                                        eM.setXml(M.getXml());
1120                                }
1121                        }
1122                }
1123        }

1125        protected static String getSpell(String word, int i)
1126        {
1127                if((word.trim().length()>0)&&((Character.isLetter(word.trim().charAt(0)))||(word.trim().startsWith("'"))||(word.trim().startsWith("`"))))
1128                {
1129                        word=word.toUpperCase().trim();
1130                        if((word.startsWith("'"))||(word.startsWith("`")))
1131                                word=word.substring(1);
1132                        if(word.length()<3)
1133                                return "";
1134                        if(word.startsWith("NONE"))
1135                                i=-1;
1136                        else
1137                        if(word.startsWith("COMPLETE HEAL"))
1138                                i=209;
1139                        else
1140                        if(word.startsWith("RESTORE MANA"))
1141                                i=234;
1142                        else
1143                        if(word.startsWith("ACID B"))
1144                                i=70;
1145                        else
1146                        if(word.startsWith("ARMOR"))
1147                                i=1;
1148                        else
1149                        if(word.startsWith("ENHANCED ARMOR"))
1150                                i=212;
1151                        else
1152                        if(word.startsWith("ENHANCE ARMOR"))
1153                                i=212;
1154                        else
1155                        if(word.startsWith("BLESS"))
1156                                i=3;
1157                        else
1158                        if(word.startsWith("BLINDNE"))
1159                                i=4;
1160                        else
1161                        if(word.startsWith("BURNING H"))

2304
2305        protected static int importNumber(String s)
2306        {
2307                final StringBuffer str=new StringBuffer("");
2308                for(int i=0;i<s.length();i++)
2309                        switch(s.charAt(i))
2310                        {
2311                        case '0':
2312                        case '1':
2313                        case '2':
2314                        case '3':
2315                        case '4':
2316                        case '5':
2317                        case '6':
2318                        case '7':
2319                        case '8':
2320                        case '9':
2321                                str.append(s.charAt(i));
2322                                break;
2323                        case 'x':
2324                        case 'X':
2325                        case 'Z':
2326                        case ' ':
2327                                break;
2328                        default:
2329                                return 0;
2330                        }
2331                return CMath.s_int(str.toString());
2332        }
2333
2334        protected static void readBlocks(
2335                                                   List<String> buf,
2336                                                   List<String> areaData,
2337                                                   List<List<String>> roomData,
2338                                                   List<String> mobData,
2339                                                   List<String> resetData,
2340                                                   List<String> objectData,
2341                                                   List<String> mobProgData,
2342                                                   List<String> objProgData,
2343                                                   List<String> shopData,
2344                                                   List<String> specialData,
2345                                                   List<String> socialData,
2346                                                   List<String> roomProgData)
2347        {
2348                final List<String> helpsToEat=new Vector<String>();
2349
2350                List wasUsingThisOne=null;
2351                List<String> useThisOne=null;
2352                while(buf.size()>0)
2353                {
2354                        String s=buf.get(0).toUpperCase().trim();
2355                        if(s.startsWith("#")&&buf.get(0).startsWith(" "))
2356                                s=buf.get(0).toUpperCase();
2357
2358                        if((useThisOne==areaData)&&(s.length()==0))
2359                        {
2360                                buf.remove(0);
2361                                continue;
2362                        }
2363
2364                        boolean okString=true;
2365                        if(s.startsWith("#"))
2366                        {
2367                                s=s.substring(1).trim();
2368                                if((useThisOne==areaData)&&(s.length()>0)&&(CMath.isInteger(s)||Character.isDigit(s.charAt(s.length()-1))))
2369                                {
2370                                        wasUsingThisOne=mobData;
2371                                        useThisOne=mobData;
2372                                }
2373
2374                                if((s.startsWith("AREA"))
2375                                ||(s.startsWith("AUTHOR")))
2376                                {
2377                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2378                                        if((s.indexOf('~')>=0)
2379                                        &&(s.startsWith("AREA ")||s.startsWith("AUTHOR ")))
2380                                                okString=true;
2381                                        useThisOne=areaData;
2382                                }
2383                                else
2384                                if((s.startsWith("MOBILE"))
2385                                ||(s.startsWith("MOBOLD")))
2386                                {
2387                                        wasUsingThisOne=mobData;
2388                                        useThisOne=mobData;
2389                                }
2390                                else
2391                                if((s.startsWith("OBJECT"))
2392                                ||(s.startsWith("OBJOLD"))
2393                                ||(s.startsWith("OBJ24B3")))
2394                                {
2395                                        wasUsingThisOne=objectData;
2396                                        useThisOne=objectData;
2397                                }
2398                                else
2399                                if((s.startsWith("OLIMITS"))
2400                                ||(s.startsWith("OMPROGS"))
2401                                ||(s.startsWith("ECONOMY"))
2402                                ||(s.startsWith("RANGES"))
2403                                ||(s.startsWith("CLIMATE"))
2404                                ||(s.startsWith("RESETMSG"))
2405                                ||(s.startsWith("VERSION"))
2406                                ||(s.startsWith("CONTINENT"))
2407                                ||(s.startsWith("COORDS"))
2408                                ||(s.startsWith("RESETFREQUENCY"))
2409                                ||(s.startsWith("VNUMS"))
2410                                ||(s.startsWith("FLAGS"))
2411                                ||(s.startsWith("REPAIRS"))
2412                                ||(s.startsWith("OBJFUNS"))
2413                                ||(s.startsWith("HELPS"))
2414                                ||(s.startsWith("PRACTICERS")))
2415                                {
2416                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2417                                        useThisOne=helpsToEat;
2418                                }
2419                                else
2420                                if(s.startsWith("MOBPROG"))
2421                                {
2422                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2423                                        useThisOne=mobProgData;
2424                                }
2425                                else
2426                                if(s.startsWith("ROOMPROG"))
2427                                {
2428                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2429                                        useThisOne=roomProgData;
2430                                }
2431                                else
2432                                if(s.startsWith("ROOM"))
2433                                {
2434                                        wasUsingThisOne=roomData;
2435                                        useThisOne=new Vector<String>();
2436                                }
2437                                else
2438                                if(s.startsWith("RESETS"))
2439                                {
2440                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2441                                        useThisOne=resetData;
2442                                }
2443                                else
2444                                if(s.startsWith("SHOP"))
2445                                {
2446                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2447                                        useThisOne=shopData;
2448                                }
2449                                else
2450                                if(s.startsWith("SPECIALS"))
2451                                {
2452                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2453                                        useThisOne=specialData;
2454                                }
2455                                else
2456                                if(s.startsWith("SOCIALS"))
2457                                {
2458                                        wasUsingThisOne=null;
2459                                        useThisOne=socialData;
2460                                }
2461                                else
2462                                if(((importNumber(s)>0)||(s.equals("0") && (buf.size()>1) && (buf.get(1).indexOf('~')>0)))
2463                                &&(wasUsingThisOne!=null))
2464                                {
2465                                        final List<String> V=new Vector<String>();
2466                                        wasUsingThisOne.add(V);
2467                                        useThisOne=V;
2468                                }
2469                                else
2470                                if(s.equals("0")||s.equals("$")||s.equals("O"))
2471                                        okString=false;
2472                                else
2473                                if((s.equals("")||s.equals("~"))&&(useThisOne==socialData))
2474                                        okString=true;
2475                                else
2476                                if((useThisOne==mobProgData)||(useThisOne==roomProgData))
2477                                        okString=true;
2478                                else
2479                                {
2480                                        //useThisOne=null;
2481                                        Log.sysOut("Import","Suspect line (probably ok="+(useThisOne!=null)+"): "+s);
2482                                }
2483                        }
2484                        if(useThisOne!=null)
2485                        {
2486                                if(okString)
2487                                        useThisOne.add(CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(buf.get(0)));
2488                                buf.remove(0);
2489                        }
2490                        else
2491                        {
2492                                Log.sysOut("Import","Just eating: "+s);
2493                                buf.remove(0);
2494                        }
2495                }
2496                if(helpsToEat.size()>0)
2497                {
2498                        Log.sysOut("Import","Ate "+helpsToEat.size()+" unsupported lines.");
2499                        helpsToEat.clear();
2500                }
2501        }
2502
2503        protected static void doWeapon(Weapon I, String name, int val1, String str1, int val2, int val3, int val4, String str4)
2504        {
2505                final String[][] weaponTypes={
2506                        { "exotic","0"},
2507                        { "sword","1"},
2508                        { "dagger","9"},
2509                        { "spear","3"},
2510                        { "staff","10"},
2511                        { "mace","4"},
2512                        { "axe","5"},
2513                        { "flail","6"},
2514                        { "whip","7"},
2515                        { "polearm","8"},
2516                        { "bow","0"},
2517                        { "arrow","3"},
2518                        {
2519                                "lance","3"
2520                        }
2521                };
2522                str1=str1.toLowerCase().trim();
2523                if(str1.startsWith("'"))
2524                        str1=str1.substring(1);
2525                for (final String[] weaponDamageType : weaponTypes)
2526                {
2527                        if(str1.startsWith(weaponDamageType[0]))
2528                        {
2529                                val1 = CMath.s_int(weaponDamageType[1]);
2530                                break;
2531                        }
2532                }
2533                if(val1==0)
2534                {
2535                        for (final String[] weaponDamageType : weaponTypes)
2536                        {
2537                                if(name.toLowerCase().indexOf(weaponDamageType[0])>=0)
2538                                {
2539                                        val1 = CMath.s_int(weaponDamageType[1]);
2540                                        break;
2541                                }
2542                        }
2543                }
2544                if((name.toUpperCase().endsWith("HAMMER"))&&(val1==4))
2545                        val1=11;
2546                switch(val1)
2547                {
2548                case 0:
2549                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_RANGED);
2550                        if (name.toUpperCase().indexOf("BOW") >= 0)
2551                        {
2552                                if (I instanceof AmmunitionWeapon)
2553                                {
2554                                        ((AmmunitionWeapon) I).setAmmoCapacity(20);
2555                                        ((AmmunitionWeapon) I).setAmmoRemaining(20);
2556                                        ((AmmunitionWeapon) I).setAmmunitionType("arrows");
2557                                }
2558                                I.setRanges(1, 3);
2559                                I.setRawLogicalAnd(true);
2560                        }
2561                        break;
2562                case 1:
2563                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_SWORD);
2564                        break;
2565                case 2:
2566                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_EDGED);
2567                        break;
2568                case 3:
2569                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_POLEARM);
2570                        I.setRanges(0, 1);
2571                        I.setRawLogicalAnd(true);
2572                        break;
2573                case 4:
2574                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_BLUNT);
2575                        break;
2576                case 5:
2577                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_AXE);
2578                        break;
2579                case 6:
2580                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_FLAILED);
2581                        I.setRanges(0, 1);
2582                        break;
2583                case 7:
2584                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_FLAILED);
2585                        I.setRanges(0, 1);
2586                        break;
2587                case 8:
2588                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_POLEARM);
2589                        I.setRanges(0, 1);
2590                        I.setRawLogicalAnd(true);
2591                        break;
2592                case 9:
2593                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_DAGGER);
2594                        break;
2595                case 10:
2596                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_STAFF);
2597                        break;
2598                case 11:
2599                        I.setWeaponClassification(Weapon.CLASS_HAMMER);
2600                        break;
2601                }
2602                if(val2>=1)
2603                        I.basePhyStats().setDamage(val2*val3);
2604                else
2605                        I.basePhyStats().setDamage(val3);
2606                if((str4.trim().length()>0)&&((Character.isLetter(str4.trim().charAt(0)))||(str4.trim().startsWith("'"))))
2607                {
2608                        str4=str4.toUpperCase().trim();
2609                        if(str4.startsWith("'"))
2610                                str4=str4.substring(1);
2611                        if(str4.startsWith("POUND"))
2612                                val4=7;
2613                        else
2614                        if(str4.startsWith("CRUSH"))
2615                                val4=7;
2616                        else
2617                        if(str4.startsWith("SMASH"))
2618                                val4=7;
2619                        else
2620                        if(str4.startsWith("FLAMI"))
2621                                val4=57;
2622                        else
2623                        if(str4.startsWith("SCORC"))
2624                                val4=57;
2625                        else
2626                        if(str4.startsWith("SEARI"))
2627                                val4=57;
2628                        else
2629                        if(str4.startsWith("GOUT"))
2630                                val4=57;
2631                        else
2632                        if(str4.startsWith("SCRATCH"))
2633                                val4=22;
2634                        else
2635                        if(str4.startsWith("CLAW"))
2636                                val4=22;
2637                        else
2638                        if(str4.startsWith("BITE"))
2639                                val4=22;
2640                        else
2641                        if(str4.startsWith("PECK"))
2642                                val4=22;
2643                        else
2644                        if(str4.startsWith("STING"))
2645                                val4=22;
2646                        else
2647                        if(str4.startsWith("BEAT"))
2648                                val4=22;
2649                        else
2650                        if(str4.startsWith("SLAP"))
2651                                val4=22;
2652                        else
2653                        if(str4.startsWith("PUNC"))
2654                                val4=22;
2655                        else
2656                        if(str4.startsWith("WHALL"))
2657                                val4=22;
2658                        else
2659                        if(str4.startsWith("STAB"))
2660                                val4=2;
2661                        else
2662                        if(str4.startsWith("PIERCE"))
2663                                val4=2;
2664                        else
2665                        if(str4.startsWith("CHOP"))
2666                                val4=25;
2667                        else
2668                        if(str4.startsWith("CLEA"))
2669                                val4=25;
2670                        else
2671                        if(str4.startsWith("SLIC"))
2672                                val4=25;
2673                        else
2674                        if(str4.startsWith("SLAS"))
2675                                val4=25;
2676                        else
2677                        if(str4.startsWith("WHIP"))
2678                                val4=25;
2679                }
2680                switch(val4)
2681                {
2682                case 7:
2683                case 8:
2684                case 27:
2685                        I.setWeaponDamageType(Weapon.TYPE_BASHING);
2686                        break;
2687                case 29:
2688                case 55:
2689                case 56:
2690                case 57:
2691                        I.setWeaponDamageType(Weapon.TYPE_BURNING);
2692                        break;
2693                case 22:
2694                case 5:
2695                case 10:
2696                case 23:
2697                case 26:
2698                case 32:
2699                case 13:
2700                case 16:
2701                case 17:
2702                case 24:
2703                        I.setWeaponDamageType(Weapon.TYPE_NATURAL);
2704                        break;
2705                case 2:
2706                case 11:
2707                        I.setWeaponDamageType(Weapon.TYPE_PIERCING);
2708                        break;
2709                case 25:
2710                case 21:
2711                case 4:
2712                case 3:
2713                case 1:
2714                        I.setWeaponDamageType(Weapon.TYPE_SLASHING);
2715                        break;
2716
2717                default:
2718                        I.setWeaponDamageType(Weapon.TYPE_BURSTING);
2719                        break;
2720                }
2721        }
2722
2723        public static int getDRoll(String str)
2724        {
2725                int i=str.indexOf('d');
2726                if(i<0)
2727                        return CMProps.getMobHPBase();
2728                final int roll=CMath.s_int(str.substring(0,i).trim());
2729                str=str.substring(i+1).trim();
2730
2731                i=str.indexOf('+');
2732                int dice=0;
2733                int plus=0;
2734                if(i<0)
2735                {
2736                        i=str.indexOf('-');
2737                        if(i<0)
2738                                dice=CMath.s_int(str.trim());
2739                        else
2740                        {
2741                                dice=CMath.s_int(str.substring(0,i).trim());
2742                                plus=CMath.s_int(str.substring(i));
2743                        }
2744                }
2745                else
2746                {
2747                        dice=CMath.s_int(str.substring(0,i).trim());
2748                        plus=CMath.s_int(str.substring(i+1));
2749                }
2750                return (roll*dice)+plus;
2751        }

3808                                                M.addBehavior(B);
3809                                        }

3812                                                M.addBehavior(CMClass.getBehavior("ROMPatrolman"));
3813                                        else
3814                                                returnAnError(session,"Unknown mob special: "+special,compileErrors,commands);
3815                                }
3816                                else
3817                                if((s.startsWith("#SPE"))||(s.startsWith("S"))||(s.startsWith("*")||(s.startsWith("#$"))||(s.startsWith("R "))))
3818                                {
3819                                }
3820                                else
3821                                if(s.trim().length()>0)
3822                                        returnAnError(session,"Unknown mob special line: "+s,compileErrors,commands);
3823                        }

3825                        {
3826                                final Ability A=M.fetchAbility(a);
3827                                if(A!=null)
3828                                        A.autoInvocation(M, false);
3829                        }
3830                        long rejuv=CMProps.getTicksPerMinute()+CMProps.getTicksPerMinute()+(CMProps.getTicksPerMinute()*M.basePhyStats().level()/2);
3831                        if(rejuv>(30*CMProps.getTicksPerMinute()))
3832                                rejuv=(30*CMProps.getTicksPerMinute());

3835                                M.addBehavior(CMClass.getBehavior("MoneyChanger"));
3836                        Behavior B=M.fetchBehavior("CombatAbilities");
3837                        if(B!=null)
3838                        {
3839                                final Behavior BB=B;
3840                                for(final Enumeration<Behavior> e=M.behaviors();e.hasMoreElements();)
3841                                {
3842                                        B=e.nextElement();
3843                                        if((B!=null)&&(B.getClass().getSuperclass().getName().endsWith("CombatAbilities")))
3844                                        {
3845                                                M.delBehavior(BB);
3846                                                M.recoverPhyStats();
3847                                                break;
3848                                        }
3849                                }
3850                        }
3851                        M.recoverCharStats();
3852                        M.recoverPhyStats();
3853                        M.recoverMaxState();
3854                        M.resetToMaxState();
3855                        M.text();
3856                        if(OfThisID.startsWith("#"))
3857                                doneMOBS.put(OfThisID.substring(1),(MOB)M.copyOf());
3858                        else
3859                                doneMOBS.put(OfThisID,(MOB)M.copyOf());
3860                        return M;
3861                }
3862                return null;
3863        }

3865        private static void applyItemApplyCode(String codesLine, Item I, Environmental adjuster, Environmental caster, Environmental resister)
3866        {
3867                final int num=CMath.s_int(CMParms.getCleanBit(codesLine,0).trim());
3868                final int val=CMath.s_int(CMParms.getCleanBit(codesLine,1).trim());
3869                switch(num)
3870                {
3871                case 1:
3872                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" str"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3873                        break;
3874                case 2:
3875                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" dex"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3876                        break;
3877                case 3:
3878                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" int"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3879                        break;
3880                case 4:
3881                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" wis"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3882                        break;
3883                case 5:
3884                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" con"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3885                        break;
3886                case 6:
3887                        // coffeemud don't play with sex
3888                        break;
3889                case 7:
3890                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" cha"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3891                        break;
3892                case 8:
3893                        break;
3894                case 9:
3895                        break;
3896                case 10:
3897                        break;
3898                case 11:
3899                        break;
3900                case 12:
3901                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" mana"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3902                        break;
3903                case 13:
3904                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" hit"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3905                        break;
3906                case 14:
3907                        adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" move"+((val>=0)?("+"+val):(""+val)));
3908                        break;
3909                case 15:
3910                        break;
3911                case 16:
3912                        break;
3913                case 17:
3914                        if((val>0)&&(I instanceof Armor))
3915                                I.basePhyStats().setArmor(I.basePhyStats().armor()+(val*5));
3916                        else
3917                                adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" armor"+((val>=0)?("+"+(val*5)):(""+(val*5))));
3918                        break;
3919                case 18:
3920                        if((val>0)&&(I instanceof Weapon))
3921                                I.basePhyStats().setAttackAdjustment(I.basePhyStats().attackAdjustment()+(val*5));
3922                        else
3923                                adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" attack"+((val>=0)?("+"+(val*5)):(""+(val*5))));
3924                        break;
3925                case 19:
3926                        if((val>0)&&(I instanceof Weapon))
3927                                I.basePhyStats().setDamage(I.basePhyStats().damage()+val);
3928                        else
3929                                adjuster.setMiscText(adjuster.text()+" damage"+((val>=0)?("+"+(val)):(""+(val))));
3930                        break;
3931                case 20: // spells, but with a numeric value.. ?!?!
3932                        break;
3933                case 21:
3934                        break;
3935                case 22:
3936                        break;
3937                case 23:
3938                        break;
3939                case 24:
3940                        resister.setMiscText(resister.text()+" magic "+((-val)*2)+"%");
3941                        break;
3942                case 25:
3943                        // i have no idea what a power up is
3944                        break;
3945                case 30:
3946                        switch(val)
3947                        {
3948                        case 6:
3949                                caster.setMiscText(caster.text()+("Prayer_Curse")+";");
3950                                break;
3951                        case 9:
3952                                caster.setMiscText(caster.text()+("Poison")+";");
3953                                break;
3954                        case 10:
3955                                caster.setMiscText(caster.text()+("Prayer_Plague")+";");
3956                                break;
3957                        case 11:
3958                                caster.setMiscText(caster.text()+("Spell_Blindness")+";");
3959                                break;
3960                        }
3961                        break;
3962                }
3963        }
