3965        private static Item getItem(String OfThisID,
3966                                                                Session session,
3967                                                                String areaName,
3968                                                                List objectData,
3969                                                                List objProgData,
3970                                                                Map<String,Item> areaItems,
3971                                                                Map<String,Item> doneItems,
3972                                                                Map<String,Room> areaRooms,
3973                                                                Map<String,Room> doneRooms,
3974                                                                boolean compileErrors,
3975                                                                List<Object> commands)
3976        {
3977                if(OfThisID.startsWith("#"))
3978                {
3979                        if(areaItems.containsKey(OfThisID.substring(1)))
3980                                return (Item)(areaItems.get(OfThisID.substring(1))).copyOf();
3981                        if(doneItems.containsKey(OfThisID.substring(1)))
3982                                return (Item)(doneItems.get(OfThisID.substring(1))).copyOf();
3983                }
3984                else
3985                {
3986                        if(areaItems.containsKey(OfThisID))
3987                                return (Item)(areaItems.get(OfThisID)).copyOf();
3988                        if(doneItems.containsKey(OfThisID))
3989                                return (Item)(doneItems.get(OfThisID)).copyOf();
3990                }
3991                for(int o=0;o<objectData.size();o++)
3992                {
3993                        List<String> objV=null;
3994                        if(objectData.get(o) instanceof List)
3995                                objV=(List)objectData.get(o);
3996                        else
3997                        if(objectData.get(o) instanceof String)
3998                        {
3999                                final String s=(String)objectData.get(o);
4000                                if((!s.toUpperCase().trim().startsWith("#OBJ"))&&(s.length()>0))
4001                                        returnAnError(session,"Eating immaterial line: "+objectData.get(o)+", area="+areaName,compileErrors,commands);
4002                                continue;
4003                        }
4004                        else
4005                                continue;
4006                        final String objectID=eatNextLine(objV);
4007                        if(isBadID(objectID))
4008                        {
4009                                Log.errOut("IMPORT","Eating bad object id "+objectID);
4010                                objectData.remove(o);
4011                                o--;
4012                                continue;
4013                        }
4014
4015                        if(!objectID.equals(OfThisID))
4016                                continue;
4017
4018                        final String simpleName=CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(eatLineSquiggle(objV));
4019                        String objectName=CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(eatLineSquiggle(objV));
4020                        final String objectDisplay=CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(eatLineSquiggle(objV));
4021                        String objectDescription="";
4022                        if((nextLine(objV).indexOf('~')>=0)||((nextLine(objV).length()>0)&&(!Character.isDigit(nextLine(objV).charAt(0)))))
4023                                objectDescription=CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(eatLineSquiggle(objV));
4024                        
4025                        String codeStr1=eatNextLine(objV);
4026                        String codeStr2=eatNextLine(objV);
4027                        String codeStr3=eatNextLine(objV);
4028                        
4029                        if((CMParms.numBits(codeStr1)==1)
4030                        &&CMath.isNumber(codeStr1)
4031                        &&(CMParms.numBits(codeStr2)==1)
4032                        &&CMath.isNumber(codeStr2))
4033                        {
4034                                //TODO: BZ: Figure out what codeStr1 & 2 are
4035                                codeStr1=codeStr3;
4036                                codeStr2=eatNextLine(objV);
4037                                codeStr3=eatNextLine(objV);
4038                        }
4039
4040                        if((!objectID.startsWith("#"))
4041                        ||((objectName.length()==0)
4042                        &&((CMParms.numBits(codeStr1)<3)
4043                        ||(CMParms.numBits(codeStr1)>4)
4044                        ||(CMParms.numBits(codeStr2)<4)
4045                        ||(codeStr3.length()==0))))
4046                        {
4047                                returnAnError(session,"Malformed object! Aborting this object "+objectID+", display="+objectDisplay+", simple="+simpleName+", name="+objectName+", codeStr1="+codeStr1+", codeStr2="+codeStr2+", codeStr3="+codeStr3+", area="+areaName,compileErrors,commands);
4048                                continue;
4049                        }
4050                        if(objectName.length()==0)
4051                                objectName="Unknown";
4052                        boolean circleForm=false;
4053                        final String obj=CMParms.getBit(codeStr1,0);
4054                        if((obj.trim().length()>1)&&(Character.isLetter(obj.charAt(0))))
4055                                circleForm=true;
4056                        int objType=CMath.s_int(obj);
4057                        final String[][] itemTypes={
4058                        { "light","1"},
4059                        { "scroll","2"},
4060                        { "wand","3"},
4061                        { "staff","4"},
4062                        { "weapon","5"},
4063                        { "treasure","8"},
4064                        { "armor","9"},
4065                        { "potion","10"},
4066                        { "clothing","11"},
4067                        { "furniture","12"},
4068                        { "trash","13"},
4069                        { "container","15"},
4070                        { "drink","17"},
4071                        { "key","18"},
4072                        { "food","19"},
4073                        { "money","20"},
4074                        { "boat","22"},
4075                        { "npc_corpse","99"},
4076                        { "pc_corpse","99"},
4077                        { "fountain","25"},
4078                        { "pill","26"},
4079                        { "protect",""},
4080                        { "map","28"},
4081                        { "portal","97"},
4082                        { "warp_stone",""},
4083                        { "room_key","98"},
4084                        { "gem",""},
4085                        { "jewelry",""},
4086                        { "jukebox",""},
4087                        { "tattoo",""},
4088                        {
4089                                "pipe","32"
4090                        }
4091                        };
4092
4093                        if(circleForm)
4094                        {
4095                                if(obj.equalsIgnoreCase("jukebox"))
4096                                        continue;// NO JUKE BOXES!
4097                                for (final String[] itemType : itemTypes)
4098                                        if(obj.equalsIgnoreCase(itemType[0]))
4099                                        {
4100                                                objType=CMath.s_int(itemType[1]);
4101                                                break;
4102                                        }
4103                        }
4104                        final long extraFlag=getBitMask(codeStr1,1);
4105                        final long wearFlag=getBitMask(codeStr1,2);
4106
4107                        Ability adjuster=CMClass.getAbility("Prop_HaveAdjuster");
4108                        switch(objType)
4109                        {
4110                        case 2:
4111                        case 3:
4112                        case 4:
4113                        case 10:
4114                                if((codeStr2.indexOf('`')<=0)
4115                                &&(nextLine(objV).indexOf('`')>=0))
4116                                        codeStr2=eatNextLine(objV);
4117                                break;
4118                        default:
4119                                break;
4120                        }
4121                        boolean forgiveZeroes=false;
4122                        if((codeStr2.indexOf('~')>=0)&&(codeStr2.lastIndexOf('~')>codeStr2.indexOf('~')))
4123                        {
4124                                final List<String> V=CMParms.parseSquiggles(codeStr2);
4125                                if(V.size()==4)
4126                                {
4127                                        forgiveZeroes=true;
4128                                        codeStr2="'"+(V.get(0))+"' "
4129                                                        +"'"+(V.get(1))+"' "
4130                                                        +"'"+(V.get(2))+"' "
4131                                                        +"'"+(V.get(3))+"'";
4132                                }
4133                                else
4134                                        returnAnError(session,"Invalid object codeStr2 line: "+codeStr2+", item not aborted, but stuff will be wrong!",compileErrors,commands);
4135                        }
4136
4137                        final String str1=CMParms.getBit(codeStr2,0);
4138                        final String str2=CMParms.getBit(codeStr2,1);
4139                        String str3=CMParms.getBit(codeStr2,2);
4140                        final String str4=CMParms.getBit(codeStr2,3);
4141                        final int val1=(int)getBitMask(codeStr2,0);
4142                        final int val2=(int)getBitMask(codeStr2,1);
4143                        final int val3=(int)getBitMask(codeStr2,2);
4144                        final int val4=(int)getBitMask(codeStr2,3);
4145                        Item I=null;
4146                        switch(objType)
4147                        {
4148                        case 1:
4149                                if (objectName.toUpperCase().indexOf("LANTERN") >= 0)
4150                                        I = CMClass.getBasicItem("GenLantern");
4151                                else
4152                                        I = CMClass.getBasicItem("GenLightSource");
4153                                ((Light) I).setDuration(val3 * 80);
4154                                break;
4155                        case 2:
4156                                I = CMClass.getMiscMagic("GenScroll");
4157                                I.basePhyStats().setLevel(val1);
4158                                I.setUsesRemaining(3);
4159                                ((SpellHolder) I).setSpellList(getSpell(str2, val2) + ";" + getSpell(str3, val3) + ";" + getSpell(str4, val4));
4160                                break;
4161                        case 3:
4162                                I = CMClass.getMiscMagic("GenWand");
4163                                I.basePhyStats().setLevel(val1);
4164                                I.setUsesRemaining(val2);
4165                                ((Wand) I).setSpell(CMClass.getAbility(getSpell(str4, val4)));
4166                                break;
4167                        case 4:
4168                                I = CMClass.getWeapon("GenStaff");
4169                                I.basePhyStats().setLevel(val1);
4170                                I.setUsesRemaining(val2);
4171                                ((Wand) I).setSpell(CMClass.getAbility(getSpell(str4, val4)));
4172                                adjuster = CMClass.getAbility("Prop_WearAdjuster");
4173                                break;
4174                        case 5:
4175                                I = CMClass.getWeapon("GenWeapon");
4176                                doWeapon((Weapon) I, objectName, val1, str1, val2, val3, val4, str4);
4177                                adjuster = CMClass.getAbility("Prop_WearAdjuster");
4178                                break;
4179                        case 6:
4180                                I = CMClass.getWeapon("GenWeapon");
4181                                doWeapon((Weapon) I, objectName, val1, str1, val2, val3, val4, str4);
4182                                adjuster = CMClass.getAbility("Prop_WearAdjuster");
4183                                break;
4184                        case 7:
4185                                I = CMClass.getWeapon("GenWeapon");
4186                                doWeapon((Weapon) I, objectName, val1, str1, val2, val3, val4, str4);
4187                                adjuster = CMClass.getAbility("Prop_WearAdjuster");
4188                                break;
4189                        case 8:
4190                                I = CMClass.getBasicItem("GenItem");
4191                                break;
4192                        case 9:
4193                                if (objectName.toUpperCase().indexOf("SHIELD") >= 0)
4194                                        I = CMClass.getArmor("GenShield");
4195                                else
4196                                        I = CMClass.getArmor("GenArmor");
4197                                I.basePhyStats().setArmor((int) Math.round(CMath.div((val1 + val2 + val3 + val4 + 1), 4.0) + 1));
4198                                adjuster = CMClass.getAbility("Prop_WearAdjuster");
4199                                break;
4200                        case 10:

4802                                                }
4803                                                else
4804                                                {

4829                                                                        resister.setMiscText(resister.text()+resistances[rei]+" 25%");
4830                                                                else

4832                                                                        resister.setMiscText(resister.text()+resistances[rei]+" 100%");

4838                                                        //if(CMath.isSet(res,18)) no sound resistance
4839                                                }
4840
4841                                        }
4842                                }
4843                                else
4844                                if(codeLine.startsWith(">"))
4845                                {
4846                                        codeLine=eatLineSquiggle(objV);
4847                                        String scriptStuff="";
4848                                        if(!codeLine.substring(1).trim().toUpperCase().startsWith("IN_FILE_PROG"))
4849                                        {
4850                                                scriptStuff+=codeLine.substring(1).trim()+";";
4851                                                codeLine=nextLine(objV);
4852                                                while(codeLine.indexOf('~')<0)
4853                                                {
4854                                                        scriptStuff+=codeLine.trim()+";";
4855                                                        eatLine(objV);
4856                                                        codeLine=nextLine(objV);
4857                                                }
4858                                                codeLine=eatLineSquiggle(objV).trim();
4859                                                scriptStuff+=codeLine+"~";
4860                                        }
4861                                        codeLine=scriptStuff;
4862                                        // nothing done with the script. :(
4863                                }
4864                                else
4865                                if(codeLine.equals("|"))
4866                                {
4867                                        eatNextLine(objV);
4868                                        // have no idea, but we skip it
4869                                }
4870                                else
4871                                if((forgiveZeroes)
4872                                &&(codeLine.length()>0)
4873                                &&(CMath.isNumber(""+codeLine.charAt(0)))
4874                                &&(CMParms.numBits(codeLine)>1))
4875                                {
4876                                        eatNextLine(objV);
4877                                        // eos support
4878                                }
4879                                else
4880                                if((forgiveZeroes)
4881                                &&(codeLine.endsWith("~")))
4882                                {
4883                                        eatNextLine(objV);
4884                                        // eos support
4885                                }
4886                                else
4887                                if((codeLine.startsWith("#"))||(codeLine.length()==0))
4888                                {
4889                                        eatNextLine(objV);
4890                                }
4891                                else
4892                                if(codeLine.equals("EXTRA"))
4893                                {
4894                                        eatNextLine(objV); // extra
4895                                        eatLineSquiggle(objV); // key word
4896                                        final String desc=CMLib.coffeeFilter().safetyFilter(eatLineSquiggle(objV)); // description
4897                                        I.setDescription(I.description()+desc);
4898                                        if(I.ID().equals("GenReadable"))
4899                                                I.setReadableText(fixReadableContent(I.description()));
4900                                }
4901                                else
4902                                if(codeLine.equals("APPLY"))
4903                                {
4904                                        eatNextLine(objV); // apply
4905                                        final String codesLine = eatNextLine(objV);
4906                                        if(CMParms.numBits(codesLine)!=2)
4907                                                returnAnError(session,"Malformed 'A' code for item "+objectID+", "+I.Name()+": "+codesLine+", area="+areaName,compileErrors,commands);
4908                                        else
4909                                                applyItemApplyCode(codesLine,I, adjuster, caster, resister);
4910                                }
4911                                else
4912                                if(codeLine.startsWith("A "))
4913                                {
4914                                        eatNextLine(objV); // apply
4915                                        final String codesLine = codeLine.substring(2).trim();
4916                                        if(CMParms.numBits(codesLine)!=2)
4917                                                returnAnError(session,"Malformed 'A' code for item "+objectID+", "+I.Name()+": "+codesLine+", area="+areaName,compileErrors,commands);
4918                                        else
4919                                                applyItemApplyCode(codesLine,I, adjuster, caster, resister);
4920                                }
4921                                else
4922                                {
4923                                        eatNextLine(objV);
4924                                        returnAnError(session,"Unknown code for item "+objectID+", "+I.Name()+": "+codeLine+", area="+areaName,compileErrors,commands);
4925                                }
4926                        }
4927                        if(adjuster.text().length()>0)
4928                                I.addNonUninvokableEffect(adjuster);
4929                        if(caster.text().length()>0)
4930                                I.addNonUninvokableEffect(caster);
4931                        if(resister.text().length()>0)
4932                                I.addNonUninvokableEffect(resister);
4933                        I.recoverPhyStats();
4934                        I.text();
4935                        I.recoverPhyStats();
4936                        if(OfThisID.startsWith("#"))
4937                        {
4938                                areaItems.put(OfThisID.substring(1),I);
4939                                doneItems.put(OfThisID.substring(1),I);
4940                        }
4941                        else
4942                        {
4943                                areaItems.put(OfThisID,I);
4944                                doneItems.put(OfThisID,I);
4945                        }
4946                        return I;
4947                }
4948                return null;
4949        }

5110        public static boolean isBadID(String id)
5111        {
5112                for(int i=0;i<id.length();i++)
5113                {
5114                        if(Character.isLetter(id.charAt(i)))
5115                        {
5116                                return true;
5117                        }
5118                }
5119                return false;
5120        }

5122        public static String socialFix(String str)
5123        {
5124
5125                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$n","<S-NAME>");
5126                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$N","<T-NAMESELF>");
5127                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$m","<S-HIM-HER>");
5128                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$M","<T-HIM-HER>");
5129                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$s","<S-HIS-HER>");
5130                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$S","<T-HIS-HER>");
5131                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$e","<S-HE-SHE>");
5132                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"$E","<T-HE-SHE>");
5133                str=CMStrings.replaceAll(str,"`","\'");
5134                if(str.equals("$"))
5135                        return "";
5136                return str.trim();
5137        }

5139        public boolean executeImporter(MOB mob, List<Object> commands) throws java.io.IOException
5140        {
5141                boolean prompt=true;
5142                boolean nodelete=false;
5143                final Map<String,Item> doneItems=new Hashtable<String,Item>();
5144                final Hashtable<String,Room> doneRooms=new Hashtable<String,Room>();
5145                final Hashtable<String,MOB> doneMOBS=new Hashtable<String,MOB>();
5146                final Vector<String> nextResetData=new Vector<String>();
5147                final Hashtable<String,String> laterLinks=new Hashtable<String,String>();
5148                boolean multiArea=false;
5149                final List<CMObject> custom=new Vector<CMObject>();
5150                final Hashtable<String,String> externalFiles=new Hashtable<String,String>();
5151                final Set<String> customBotherChecker=new HashSet<String>();
5152                boolean compileErrors=false;
5153                String areaType=null;
5154                commands.remove(0);
5155                for(int i=0;i<commands.size();i++)
5156                {
5157                        if(commands.get(i) instanceof String)
5158                        {
5159                                String s=(String)commands.get(i);
5160                                if(s.equalsIgnoreCase("nodelete"))
5161                                {
5162                                        commands.remove(i);
5163                                        i--;
5164                                        nodelete=true;
5165                                }
5166                                else
5167                                if(s.equalsIgnoreCase("noprompt"))
5168                                {
5169                                        commands.remove(i);
5170                                        i--;
5171                                        prompt=false;
5172                                }
5173                                else
5174                                if(s.toLowerCase().startsWith("areatype="))
5175                                {
5176                                        s=s.substring(9);
5177                                        if(CMClass.getAreaType(s)!=null)
5178                                                areaType=s;
5179                                        else
5180                                        {
5181                                                mob.tell(L("Unknown area type : @x1",s));
5182                                                return false;
5183                                        }
5184                                        commands.remove(i);
5185                                        i--;
5186                                }
5187                                else
5188                                        break;
5189                        }
5190                        else
5191                                break;
5192                }
5193                Session session=mob.session();
5194                if((commands.size()>0)&&(commands.get(commands.size()-1) instanceof StringBuffer))
5195                {
5196                        compileErrors=true;
5197                        session=null;
5198                }
5199                else
5200                {
5201                        if(session==null)
5202                                return false;
5203                        if(commands.size()<1)
5204                                return returnAnError(session,"Import what?  Specify the path/filename!",compileErrors,commands);
5205                        // continue pre-processing
5206                        for(int areaFile=commands.size()-1;areaFile>=0;areaFile--)
5207                        {
5208                                final String areaFileName=(String)commands.get(areaFile);
5209                                final CMFile F=new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS);
5210                                final CMFile[] FF=F.listFiles();
5211                                if((FF!=null)&&(FF.length>0))
5212                                {
5213                                        for (final CMFile element : FF)
5214                                                commands.add(element.getAbsolutePath());
5215                                        commands.remove(areaFile);
5216                                }
5217                        }
5218                }
5219
5220                final Vector mobData=new Vector(); // outside the for loop -- why?
5221                final Vector objectData=new Vector(); // outside the for loop -- why?
5222
5223                multiArea=commands.size()>1;
5224                final HashSet<String> baseFilesAlreadyDone=new HashSet<String>();
5225                while(commands.size()>0)
5226                {
5227                        final Object O=commands.remove(0);
5228                        final Vector areaData=new Vector();
5229                        final Vector roomData=new Vector();
5230                        final Vector<String> resetData=new Vector<String>();
5231                        final Vector mobProgData=new Vector();
5232                        final Vector roomProgData=new Vector();
5233                        final Vector objProgData=new Vector();
5234                        final Vector shopData=new Vector();
5235                        final Vector specialData=new Vector();
5236                        final Vector<Room> newRooms=new Vector<Room>();
5237                        final Vector<String> socialData=new Vector<String>();
5238                        Vector<String> reLinkTable=null;
5239        
5240                        StringBuffer buf=null;
5241                        String areaFileName=null;
5242                        CMFile CF=null;
5243                        boolean zonFormat=false;
5244                        if(O instanceof StringBuffer)
5245                        {
5246                                areaFileName="memory.cmare";
5247                                buf=(StringBuffer)O;
5248                        }
5249                        else
5250                        if(O instanceof Pair)
5251                        {
5252                                areaFileName=((Pair)O).first.toString();
5253                                buf=(StringBuffer)((Pair)O).second;
5254                        }
5255                        else
5256                        if(O instanceof java.util.zip.ZipInputStream)
5257                        {
5258                                final java.util.zip.ZipInputStream i=(java.util.zip.ZipInputStream)O;
5259                                final java.util.zip.ZipEntry entry=i.getNextEntry();
5260                                if(entry==null)
5261                                {
5262                                        i.close();
5263                                        continue;
5264                                }
5265                                final byte[] data = new byte[(int)entry.getSize()];
5266                                int dex=0;
5267                                int read=i.read(data);
5268                                while((read>=0)&&(dex < entry.getSize()))
5269                                {
5270                                        dex+=read;
5271                                        read=i.read(data, dex, (int)entry.getSize()-dex);
5272                                }
5273                                i.closeEntry();
5274                                if(commands.size()==0)
5275                                {
5276                                        commands.add(new Pair<String,StringBuffer>("unzip:"+entry.getName(),new StringBuffer(new String(data))));
5277                                        commands.add(i);
5278                                }
5279                                else
5280                                {
5281                                        commands.add(0,new Pair<String,StringBuffer>("unzip:"+entry.getName(),new StringBuffer(new String(data))));
5282                                        commands.add(1,i);
5283                                }
5284                                continue;
5285                        }
5286                        else
5287                        {
5288                                areaFileName=(String)O;
5289                                final int x=areaFileName.lastIndexOf('.');
5290                                final String ext=(x>0)?areaFileName.toLowerCase().substring(x+1):"";
5291                                // read in the .are file
5292        
5293                                if(ext.equalsIgnoreCase("zip"))
5294                                {
5295                                        final java.util.zip.ZipInputStream i=new java.util.zip.ZipInputStream(new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS).getRawStream());
5296                                        if(commands.size()==0)
5297                                                commands.add(i);
5298                                        else
5299                                                commands.add(0,i);
5300                                        continue;
5301                                }
5302                                if(ext.equals("zon")
5303                                || ext.endsWith("wld")
5304                                || ext.endsWith("obj")
5305                                || ext.endsWith("mob")
5306                                || ext.endsWith("shp")
5307                                || ext.endsWith("doc"))
5308                                {
5309                                        final String baseAreaFileName=areaFileName.substring(0,x);
5310                                        if(baseFilesAlreadyDone.contains(baseAreaFileName.toLowerCase()))
5311                                                continue;
5312                                        baseFilesAlreadyDone.add(baseAreaFileName.toLowerCase());
5313                                        areaFileName=baseAreaFileName+".zon";
5314                                        CF=new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS);
5315                                        buf=CF.text();
5316                                        final StringBuffer finalBuf=new StringBuffer("");
5317                                        final String eoln=CMStrings.determineEOLN(buf);
5318                                        String resetsStr="";
5319                                        if((buf!=null)&&(buf.length()>0))
5320                                        {
5321                                                final int wldDivDex=buf.indexOf(eoln+eoln);
5322                                                if(wldDivDex<0)
5323                                                        return returnAnError(session,"Malformed Zone at: '"+areaFileName+"'!",compileErrors,commands);
5324                                                int startDex=0;
5325                                                if(buf.charAt(0)=='#')
5326                                                        startDex=buf.indexOf(eoln)+eoln.length();
5327                                                finalBuf.append("#AREA").append(eoln).append(buf.substring(startDex,wldDivDex)).append(eoln).append(eoln);
5328                                                resetsStr=L("#RESETS@x1@x2@x3@x4",eoln,buf.substring(wldDivDex+(eoln.length()*2)),eoln,eoln);
5329                                                areaFileName=baseAreaFileName+".wld";
5330                                                CF=new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS);
5331                                                buf=CF.text();
5332                                        }
5333                                        if((buf!=null)&&(buf.length()>0))
5334                                        {
5335                                                finalBuf.append("#ROOMS").append(eoln).append(buf.toString()).append(eoln).append(eoln);
5336                                                areaFileName=baseAreaFileName+".mob";
5337                                                CF=new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS);
5338                                                buf=CF.text();
5339                                        }
5340                                        if((buf!=null)&&(buf.length()>0))
5341                                        {
5342                                                finalBuf.append("#MOBILES").append(eoln).append(buf.toString()).append(eoln).append(eoln);
5343                                                areaFileName=baseAreaFileName+".obj";
5344                                                CF=new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS);
5345                                                buf=CF.text();
5346                                        }

5348                                        {
5349                                                finalBuf.append("#OBJECTS").append(eoln).append(buf.toString()).append(eoln).append(eoln);
5350                                                finalBuf.append(resetsStr);
5351                                                areaFileName=baseAreaFileName+".zon";
5352                                        }

5356                                else

5358                                        CF=new CMFile(areaFileName,mob,CMFile.FLAG_LOGERRORS);
5359                                        buf=CF.text();
5360                                }

5380                                                case '\n':

5387                                                        break;
5388                                                default:

5390                                                        c++;
5391                                                        break;
5392                                                }
5393                                        }

7373                        }
7374                }
7375
7376                if(nextResetData.size()>0)
7377                {
7378                        final StringBuffer nrf=new StringBuffer("Import bad resets:\n\r");
7379                        for(int nrd=0;nrd<nextResetData.size();nrd++)
7380                                nrf.append(nextResetData.get(nrd)+"\n\r");
7381                        returnAnError(session,nrf.toString(),compileErrors,commands);
7382                        Log.errOut("Import",nrf.toString());
7383                }
7384
7385                if((doneRooms.size()>0)&&(session!=null))
7386                        session.print(L("\n\nSaving all areas imported..."));
7387                for(final Enumeration<Room> e=doneRooms.elements();e.hasMoreElements();)
7388                {
7389                        final Room saveRoom=e.nextElement();
7390                        CMLib.database().DBCreateRoom(saveRoom);
7391                        // final exit clean-up optimization
7392                        for(int d=Directions.NUM_DIRECTIONS()-1;d>=0;d--)
7393                        {
7394                                final Exit X=saveRoom.getRawExit(d);
7395                                if((X!=null)
7396                                &&(X.isGeneric())
7397                                &&(!X.hasADoor())
7398                                &&(!X.hasALock())
7399                                &&(X.name().equalsIgnoreCase("the ground"))
7400                                &&(!X.isReadable())
7401                                &&(X.numEffects()==0)
7402                                &&(X.numBehaviors()==0)
7403                                &&(X.temporaryDoorLink().length()==0)
7404                                &&(X.displayText().equals(X.description())))
7405                                {
7406                                        final Exit E2=CMClass.getExit("OpenDescriptable");
7407                                        E2.setMiscText(X.displayText());
7408                                        saveRoom.setRawExit(d,E2);
7409                                }
7410                        }
7411                        CMLib.threads().clearDebri(saveRoom,0);
7412                        CMLib.database().DBUpdateExits(saveRoom);
7413                        CMLib.database().DBUpdateMOBs(saveRoom);
7414                        CMLib.database().DBUpdateItems(saveRoom);
7415                        saveRoom.startItemRejuv();
7416                        saveRoom.recoverRoomStats();
7417                        if(session!=null)
7418                                session.print(".");
7419                }
7420                if(session!=null)
7421                        session.println("!");
7422
7423                if(laterLinks.size()>0)
7424                {
7425                        for(final Enumeration<String> e=laterLinks.keys();e.hasMoreElements();)
7426                        {
7427                                final String key=e.nextElement();
7428                                final String dcode=laterLinks.get(key);
7429                                String roomID="";
7430                                String dirID="";
7431                                final int x=key.lastIndexOf('/');
7432                                if(x>=0)
7433                                {
7434                                        roomID=key.substring(0,x);
7435                                        dirID=key.substring(x+1);
7436                                }
7437                                else
7438                                        continue;
7439
7440                                Room R1=getRoom(doneRooms,doneRooms,"NOAREA",roomID);
7441                                if(R1!=null)
7442                                {
7443                                        final int dir=CMath.s_int(dirID);
7444                                        Room RR=null;
7445                                        Exit RE=null;
7446                                        if(dir<Directions.NUM_DIRECTIONS())
7447                                        {
7448                                                RR=R1.rawDoors()[dir];
7449                                                RE=R1.getRawExit(dir);
7450                                        }
7451                                        final Room TR=getRoom(doneRooms,doneRooms,"NOAREA",dcode);
7452                                        if((RR==null)&&(TR==null))
7453                                                returnAnError(session,"Room "+R1.roomID()+" links to unknown room "+dcode+" in direction "+CMLib.directions().getDirectionName(dir)+".",compileErrors,commands);
7454                                        else
7455                                        if(RR==null)
7456                                        {
7457                                                synchronized(("SYNC"+R1.roomID()).intern())
7458                                                {
7459                                                        R1=CMLib.map().getRoom(R1);
7460                                                        R1.rawDoors()[dir]=TR;
7461                                                        if(RE!=null)
7462                                                                RE.setTemporaryDoorLink("");
7463                                                        CMLib.database().DBUpdateExits(R1);
7464                                                }
7465                                        }
7466                                }
7467                        }
7468                }
7469
7470                Area A=null;
7471                for(final Enumeration<Room> e=doneRooms.elements();e.hasMoreElements();)
7472                {
7473                        A=e.nextElement().getArea();
7474                        A.setAreaState(Area.State.ACTIVE);
7475                }
7476                if(doneRooms.elements().hasMoreElements())
7477                {
7478                        for(final Enumeration<Area> a=CMLib.map().areas();a.hasMoreElements();)
7479                                a.nextElement().fillInAreaRooms();
7480                }
7481                if(session!=null)
7482                        session.println(L("done!"));
7483                return true;
7484        }
7485
7486        @Override
7487        public boolean execute(MOB mob, List<String> commands, int metaFlags)
7488                throws java.io.IOException
7489        {
7490                final List<Object> objCommands = new Vector<Object>(commands.size());
7491                for(String s : commands)
7492                        objCommands.add(s);
7493                return executeImporter(mob,objCommands);
7494        }
7495        
7496        @Override
7497        public Object executeInternal(MOB mob, int metaFlags, Object... args) throws java.io.IOException
7498        {
7499                if(!super.checkArguments(internalParameters, args))
7500                        return Boolean.FALSE;
7501                Vector<Object> objCommands = new XVector<Object>(args);
7502                executeImporter(mob,objCommands);
7503                return objCommands;
7504        }
7505        
7506        @Override
7507        public boolean canBeOrdered()
7508        {
7509                return true;
7510        }
7511
7512        @Override
7513        public boolean securityCheck(MOB mob)
7514        {
7515                return CMSecurity.isAllowedAnywhereContainsAny(mob, CMSecurity.SECURITY_IMPORT_GROUP);
7516        }
7517}
